      function calculateAndSendPerformance () {
        setTimeout(function () {
          var performance = window.performance || window.webkitPerformance || window.msPerformance || window.mozPerformance;
          var timing = performance && performance.timing;

          if (!performance || !timing || !$nuxt) return;

          var events = [{
            PROFILER_SPA_FULL_DCL: timing.domContentLoadedEventEnd - timing.navigationStart
          }, {
            PROFILER_SPA_FULL_LOAD: timing.loadEventEnd - timing.navigationStart
          }, {
            PROFILER_SPA_DCL: timing.domContentLoadedEventEnd - timing.responseEnd
          }, {
            PROFILER_SPA_LOAD: timing.loadEventEnd - timing.responseEnd
          }, {
            PROFILER_SPA_RESPONSE: timing.responseEnd - timing.responseStart
          }];

          events = events.map(function (event) {
            const name = Object.keys( event )[ 0 ];
            return {
              name: name,
              params: {
               duration: event[ name ],
               durations: {
                 connect: timing.connectEnd - timing.navigationStart,
                 server: timing.responseStart - timing.requestStart,
                 response: timing.responseEnd - timing.responseStart,
                 client: timing.loadEventEnd - timing.responseEnd,
                 full: timing.loadEventEnd - timing.navigationStart
               },
               timing: timing
              }
            };
          });

          $nuxt.$pm.events(events).finally(function () {
            window.removeEventListener('load', calculateAndSendPerformance);
          });
        }, 0);
      }

      window.addEventListener('load', function () {
        var sendTimingEvents;

        function trySendEvents () {
          try {
            if (!window.$nuxt) {
              throw new Error('');
            }
            calculateAndSendPerformance();
            clearInterval(sendTimingEvents);
          } catch (error) {}
        }

        sendTimingEvents = setInterval(trySendEvents, 500);
      });
